  var STYLE_ID = 'at-body-style';
  function getParent() {
    return doc.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
  }
  function addStyle(parent, id, def) {
    if (!parent) {
      return;
    }

    style.id = id;
    style.innerHTML = def;
